/// ?o?n mă tham kh?o Phase 1
public void validationPhase1() {
    System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()
        .when().get("/api/resource/uuid_" + dynamicId)
        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}

** GI?I NGH?A**: Ph??ng th?c kh?i x??ng k?t n?i HTTP g?i lęn server kčm theo filter c?a Allure nh?m h?ng lu?ng I/O t? RestAssured ??y vŕo báo cáo HTML. Sau ?ó ph??ng th?c `.log().all()` th?c thi nhi?m v? Logging toŕn c?c. Bi?u th?c statusCode(200) lŕ x??ng s?ng c?a c? ch? Assertion, ngay khi response code khác thě v?ng AssertionError t? ??ng báo Fail.

    System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()

        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}

    System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()
        .when().get("/api/resource/uuid_" + dynamicId)
        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}

/// ?o?n mă tham kh?o Phase 1
public void validationPhase1() {
    System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()
        .when().get("/api/resource/uuid_" + dynamicId)
        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}

** GI?I NGH?A**: Ph??ng th?c kh?i x??ng k?t n?i HTTP g?i lęn server kčm theo filter c?a Allure nh?m h?ng lu?ng I/O t? RestAssured ??y vŕo báo cáo HTML. /// ?o?n mă tham kh?o Phase 1
public void validationPhase1() {
    System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()
        .when().get("/api/resource/uuid_" + dynamicId)
        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}

** GI?I NGH?A**: Ph??ng th?c kh?i x??ng k?t n?i HTTP g?i lęn server kčm theo filter c?a Allure nh?m h?ng lu?ng I/O t? RestAssured ??y vŕo báo cáo HTML.     System.out.println("Kh?i ??ng chu?i móc n?i giao th?c HTTP/1.1...");
    ValidatableResponse response = RestAssured.given().spec(baseSpec)
        .filter(new AllureRestAssured())
        .log().all()
        .when().get("/api/resource/uuid_" + dynamicId)
        .then().log().ifError()
        .statusCode(200)
        .time(Matchers.lessThan(2500L));

    Assert.assertNotNull(response.extract().body().asString());
}
